   134	export function loadEffectiveGSDPreferences(): LoadedGSDPreferences | null {
   135	  const globalPreferences = loadGlobalGSDPreferences();
   136	  const projectPreferences = loadProjectGSDPreferences();
   137	
   138	  if (!globalPreferences && !projectPreferences) return null;
   139	
   140	  let result: LoadedGSDPreferences;
   141	  if (!globalPreferences) {
   142	    result = projectPreferences!;
   143	  } else if (!projectPreferences) {
   144	    result = globalPreferences;
   145	  } else {
   146	    const mergedWarnings = [
   147	      ...(globalPreferences.warnings ?? []),
   148	      ...(projectPreferences.warnings ?? []),
   149	    ];
   150	    result = {
   151	      path: projectPreferences.path,
   152	      scope: "project",
   153	      preferences: mergePreferences(globalPreferences.preferences, projectPreferences.preferences),
   154	      ...(mergedWarnings.length > 0 ? { warnings: mergedWarnings } : {}),
   155	    };
   156	  }
   157	
   158	  // Apply token-profile defaults as the lowest-priority layer so that
   159	  // `token_profile: budget` sets models and phase-skips automatically.
   160	  // Explicit user preferences always override profile defaults.
   161	  const profile = result.preferences.token_profile as TokenProfile | undefined;
   162	  if (profile) {
   163	    const profileDefaults = _resolveProfileDefaults(profile);
   164	    result = {
   165	      ...result,
   166	      preferences: mergePreferences(profileDefaults as GSDPreferences, result.preferences),
   167	    };
   168	  }
   169	
   170	  // Apply mode defaults as the lowest-priority layer
   171	  if (result.preferences.mode) {
   172	    result = {
   173	      ...result,
   174	      preferences: applyModeDefaults(result.preferences.mode, result.preferences),
   175	    };
   176	  }
   177	
   178	  return result;
   179	}

     2	 * GSD bootstrappers for .gitignore and preferences.md
     3	 *
     4	 * Ensures baseline .gitignore exists with universally-correct patterns.
     5	 * Creates an empty preferences.md template if it doesn't exist.
     6	 * Both idempotent — non-destructive if already present.
     7	 */
     8	
     9	import { join } from "node:path";
    10	import { execFileSync } from "node:child_process";
    11	import { existsSync, lstatSync, readFileSync, writeFileSync } from "node:fs";
    12	import { nativeRmCached, nativeLsFiles } from "./native-git-bridge.js";
    13	import { gsdRoot } from "./paths.js";
    14	import { GIT_NO_PROMPT_ENV } from "./git-constants.js";
    15	
    16	/**
    17	 * GSD runtime patterns for git index cleanup.
    18	 * With external state (symlink), these are a no-op in most cases,
    19	 * but retained for backwards compatibility during migration.
    20	 */
    21	const GSD_RUNTIME_PATTERNS = [
    22	  ".gsd/activity/",
    23	  ".gsd/forensics/",
    24	  ".gsd/runtime/",
    25	  ".gsd/worktrees/",
    26	  ".gsd/parallel/",

    38	  ".gsd/milestones/**/continue.md",

    41	const BASELINE_PATTERNS = [
    42	  // ── GSD state directory (symlink to external storage) ──
    43	  ".gsd",
    44	
    45	  // ── OS junk ──
    46	  ".DS_Store",
    47	  "Thumbs.db",
    48	
    49	  // ── Editor / IDE ──

    69	  "__pycache__/",

    86	
    87	/**
    88	 * Check whether `.gsd/` contains files tracked by git.
    89	 * If so, the project intentionally keeps `.gsd/` in version control
    90	 * and we must NOT add `.gsd` to `.gitignore` or attempt migration.
    91	 *
    92	 * Returns true if git tracks at least one file under `.gsd/`.
    93	 * Returns false (safe to ignore) if:
    94	 *   - Not a git repo
    95	 *   - `.gsd/` is a symlink (external state, should be ignored)
    96	 *   - `.gsd/` doesn't exist
    97	 *   - No tracked files found under `.gsd/`
    98	 */
    99	export function hasGitTrackedGsdFiles(basePath: string): boolean {
   100	  const localGsd = join(basePath, ".gsd");
   101	
   102	  // If .gsd doesn't exist or is already a symlink, no tracked files concern
   103	  if (!existsSync(localGsd)) return false;
   104	  try {
   105	    if (lstatSync(localGsd).isSymbolicLink()) return false;
   106	  } catch {
   107	    return false;
   108	  }
   109	
   110	  // Check if git tracks any files under .gsd/
   111	  try {
   112	    const tracked = nativeLsFiles(basePath, ".gsd");
   113	    if (tracked.length > 0) return true;
   114	
   115	    // nativeLsFiles swallows git failures and returns []. An empty result
   116	    // could mean "nothing tracked" OR "git failed silently". Verify git is
   117	    // reachable before trusting the empty result — if it isn't, fail safe
   118	    // by assuming files ARE tracked to prevent data loss.
   119	    execFileSync("git", ["rev-parse", "--git-dir"], {
   120	      cwd: basePath,
   121	      stdio: "pipe",
   122	      env: GIT_NO_PROMPT_ENV,
   123	    });
   124	
   125	    return false;
   126	  } catch {
   127	    // git unavailable, index locked, or repo corrupt — fail safe
   128	    return true;
   129	  }
   130	}
   131	
   132	/**
   133	 * Ensure basePath/.gitignore contains baseline ignore patterns.
   134	 * Creates the file if missing; appends missing patterns.
   135	 * Returns true if the file was created or modified, false if already complete.
   136	 *
   137	 * **Safety check:** If `.gsd/` contains git-tracked files (i.e., the project
   138	 * intentionally keeps `.gsd/` in version control), the `.gsd` ignore pattern
   139	 * is excluded to prevent data loss. Only the `.gsd` pattern is affected —
   140	 * all other baseline patterns are still applied normally.
   141	 */
   142	export function ensureGitignore(
   143	  basePath: string,
   144	  options?: { manageGitignore?: boolean },
   145	): boolean {
   146	  // If manage_gitignore is explicitly false, do not touch .gitignore at all
   147	  if (options?.manageGitignore === false) return false;
   148	
   149	  const gitignorePath = join(basePath, ".gitignore");
   150	
   151	  let existing = "";
   152	  if (existsSync(gitignorePath)) {
   153	    existing = readFileSync(gitignorePath, "utf-8");
   154	  }
   155	
   156	  // Parse existing lines (trimmed, ignoring comments and blanks)
   157	  const existingLines = new Set(
   158	    existing
   159	      .split("\n")
   160	      .map((l) => l.trim())
   161	      .filter((l) => l && !l.startsWith("#")),
   162	  );
   163	
   164	  // Determine which patterns to apply. If .gsd/ has tracked files,
   165	  // exclude the ".gsd" pattern to prevent deleting tracked state.
   166	  const gsdIsTracked = hasGitTrackedGsdFiles(basePath);
   167	  const patternsToApply = gsdIsTracked
   168	    ? BASELINE_PATTERNS.filter((p) => p !== ".gsd")
   169	    : BASELINE_PATTERNS;
   170	
   171	  // Find patterns not yet present
   172	  const missing = patternsToApply.filter((p) => !existingLines.has(p));
   173	
   174	  if (missing.length === 0) return false;
   175	
   176	  // Build the block to append
   177	  const block = [
   178	    "",
   179	    "# ── GSD baseline (auto-generated) ──",
   180	    ...missing,
   181	    "",
   182	  ].join("\n");
   183	
   184	  // Ensure existing content ends with a newline before appending
   185	  const prefix = existing && !existing.endsWith("\n") ? "\n" : "";
   186	  writeFileSync(gitignorePath, existing + prefix + block, "utf-8");
   187	
   188	  return true;
   189	}
   190	
   191	/**
   192	 * Remove BASELINE_PATTERNS runtime paths from the git index if they are
   193	 * currently tracked. This fixes repos that started tracking these files
   194	 * before the .gitignore rule was added — git continues tracking files
   195	 * already in the index even after .gitignore is updated.
   196	 *
   197	 * Only removes from the index (`--cached`), never from disk. Idempotent.
   198	 *
   199	 * Note: These are strictly runtime/ephemeral paths (activity logs, lock files,
   200	 * metrics, STATE.md). They are always safe to untrack, even when the project
   201	 * intentionally keeps other `.gsd/` files (like PROJECT.md, milestones/) in
   202	 * version control.
   203	 */
   204	export function untrackRuntimeFiles(basePath: string): void {
   205	  const runtimePaths = GSD_RUNTIME_PATTERNS;
   206	
   207	  for (const pattern of runtimePaths) {
   208	    // Use -r for directory patterns (trailing slash), strip the slash for the command
   209	    const target = pattern.endsWith("/") ? pattern.slice(0, -1) : pattern;
   210	    try {
   211	      nativeRmCached(basePath, [target]);
   212	    } catch {
   213	      // File not tracked or doesn't exist — expected, ignore
   214	    }
   215	  }
   216	}
   217	
   218	/**
   219	 * Ensure basePath/.gsd/preferences.md exists as an empty template.
   220	 * Creates the file with frontmatter only if it doesn't exist.
   221	 * Returns true if created, false if already exists.
   222	 *
   223	 * Checks both lowercase (canonical) and uppercase (legacy) to avoid
   224	 * creating a duplicate when an uppercase file already exists.
   225	 */
   226	export function ensurePreferences(basePath: string): boolean {
   227	  const preferencesPath = join(gsdRoot(basePath), "preferences.md");
   228	  const legacyPath = join(gsdRoot(basePath), "PREFERENCES.md");
   229	
   230	  if (existsSync(preferencesPath) || existsSync(legacyPath)) {
   231	    return false;
   232	  }
   233	
   234	  const template = `---
   235	version: 1
   236	always_use_skills: []
   237	prefer_skills: []
   238	avoid_skills: []
   239	skill_rules: []
   240	custom_instructions: []
   241	models: {}
   242	skill_discovery: {}
   243	auto_supervisor: {}
   244	---
   245	
   246	# GSD Skill Preferences
   247	
   248	Project-specific guidance for skill selection and execution preferences.
   249	
   250	See \`~/.gsd/agent/extensions/gsd/docs/preferences-reference.md\` for full field documentation and examples.
   251	
   252	## Fields
   253	
   254	- \`always_use_skills\`: Skills that must be available during all GSD operations
   255	- \`prefer_skills\`: Skills to prioritize when multiple options exist
   256	- \`avoid_skills\`: Skills to minimize or avoid (with lower priority than prefer)
   257	- \`skill_rules\`: Context-specific rules (e.g., "use tool X for Y type of work")
   258	- \`custom_instructions\`: Append-only project guidance (do not override system rules)
   259	- \`models\`: Model preferences for specific task types
   260	- \`skill_discovery\`: Automatic skill detection preferences
   261	- \`auto_supervisor\`: Supervision and gating rules for autonomous modes
   262	- \`git\`: Git preferences — \`main_branch\` (default branch name for new repos, e.g., "main", "master", "trunk"), \`auto_push\`, \`snapshots\`, etc.
   263	
   264	## Examples
   265	
   266	\`\`\`yaml
   267	prefer_skills:
   268	  - playwright
   269	  - resolve_library
   270	avoid_skills:

     1	/**
     2	 * GSD Paths — ID-based path resolution
     3	 *
     4	 * Directories use bare IDs: M001/, S01/, etc.
     5	 * Files use ID-SUFFIX: M001-ROADMAP.md, S01-PLAN.md, T01-PLAN.md
     6	 *
     7	 * Resolvers still handle legacy descriptor-suffixed names
     8	 * (e.g. M001-FLIGHT-SIMULATOR/, T03-INSTALL-PACKAGES-PLAN.md)
     9	 * via prefix matching, so existing projects work without migration.
    10	 */
    11	
    12	import { readdirSync, existsSync, realpathSync, Dirent } from "node:fs";
    13	import { join, dirname, normalize } from "node:path";
    14	import { spawnSync } from "node:child_process";
    15	import { nativeScanGsdTree, type GsdTreeEntry } from "./native-parser-bridge.js";
    16	import { DIR_CACHE_MAX } from "./constants.js";
    17	
    18	// ─── Directory Listing Cache ──────────────────────────────────────────────────
    19	
    20	const dirEntryCache = new Map<string, Dirent[]>();
    21	const dirListCache = new Map<string, string[]>();
    22	
    23	// ─── Native Tree Cache ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
    24	// When the native module is available, scan the entire .gsd/ tree in one call
    25	// and serve directory listings from memory instead of individual readdirSync calls.
    26	
    27	let nativeTreeCache: Map<string, GsdTreeEntry[]> | null = null;
    28	let nativeTreeBase: string | null = null;
    29	
    30	function getNativeTree(gsdDir: string): Map<string, GsdTreeEntry[]> | null {
    31	  if (nativeTreeCache && nativeTreeBase === gsdDir) return nativeTreeCache;
    32	
    33	  const entries = nativeScanGsdTree(gsdDir);
    34	  if (!entries) return null;
    35	
    36	  // Build a map of parent directory -> entries
    37	  const tree = new Map<string, GsdTreeEntry[]>();
    38	  for (const entry of entries) {
    39	    const parts = entry.path.split('/');
    40	    const parentPath = parts.slice(0, -1).join('/');
    41	    const parentKey = parentPath || '.';
    42	    if (!tree.has(parentKey)) tree.set(parentKey, []);
    43	    tree.get(parentKey)!.push(entry);
    44	  }
    45	
    46	  nativeTreeCache = tree;
    47	  nativeTreeBase = gsdDir;
    48	  return tree;
    49	}
    50	
    51	/**
    52	 * Convert a native tree lookup into a relative key for the tree map.
    53	 * Returns the relative path from the gsdDir, or null if the path isn't under gsdDir.
    54	 */
    55	function nativeTreeKey(dirPath: string, gsdDir: string): string | null {
    56	  if (!dirPath.startsWith(gsdDir)) return null;
    57	  const rel = dirPath.slice(gsdDir.length).replace(/^\//, '');
    58	  return rel || '.';
    59	}
    60	
    61	function cachedReaddirWithTypes(dirPath: string): Dirent[] {
    62	  const cached = dirEntryCache.get(dirPath);
    63	  if (cached) return cached;
    64	
    65	  // Try native tree cache for paths under .gsd/
    66	  if (nativeTreeBase) {
    67	    const key = nativeTreeKey(dirPath, nativeTreeBase);
    68	    if (key && nativeTreeCache) {
    69	      const treeEntries = nativeTreeCache.get(key);
    70	      if (treeEntries) {
    71	        // Synthesize Dirent-like objects from native tree entries
    72	        const dirents = treeEntries.map(e => {
    73	          const d = Object.create(Dirent.prototype) as Dirent;
    74	          Object.assign(d, {
    75	            name: e.name,
    76	            parentPath: dirPath,
    77	            path: dirPath,
    78	          });
    79	          // Override the type check methods
    80	          const isDir = e.isDir;
    81	          d.isDirectory = () => isDir;
    82	          d.isFile = () => !isDir;
    83	          d.isSymbolicLink = () => false;
    84	          d.isBlockDevice = () => false;
    85	          d.isCharacterDevice = () => false;
    86	          d.isFIFO = () => false;
    87	          d.isSocket = () => false;
    88	          return d;
    89	        });
    90	        if (dirEntryCache.size >= DIR_CACHE_MAX) dirEntryCache.clear();
    91	        dirEntryCache.set(dirPath, dirents);
    92	        return dirents;
    93	      }
    94	    }
    95	  }
    96	
    97	  const entries = readdirSync(dirPath, { withFileTypes: true });
    98	  if (dirEntryCache.size >= DIR_CACHE_MAX) dirEntryCache.clear();
    99	  dirEntryCache.set(dirPath, entries);
   100	  return entries;
   101	}
   102	
   103	function cachedReaddir(dirPath: string): string[] {
   104	  const cached = dirListCache.get(dirPath);
   105	  if (cached) return cached;
   106	
   107	  // Try native tree cache for paths under .gsd/
   108	  if (nativeTreeBase) {
   109	    const key = nativeTreeKey(dirPath, nativeTreeBase);
   110	    if (key && nativeTreeCache) {
   111	      const treeEntries = nativeTreeCache.get(key);
   112	      if (treeEntries) {
   113	        const names = treeEntries.map(e => e.name);
   114	        if (dirListCache.size >= DIR_CACHE_MAX) dirListCache.clear();
   115	        dirListCache.set(dirPath, names);
   116	        return names;
   117	      }
   118	    }
   119	  }
   120	
   121	  const entries = readdirSync(dirPath);
   122	  if (dirListCache.size >= DIR_CACHE_MAX) dirListCache.clear();
   123	  dirListCache.set(dirPath, entries);
   124	  return entries;
   125	}

   285	/** Exported for tests only — do not call in production code. */
   286	export function _clearGsdRootCache(): void {
   287	  gsdRootCache.clear();
   288	}
   289	
   290	/**
   291	 * Resolve the `.gsd` directory for a given project base path.
   292	 *
   293	 * Probe order:
   294	 *   1. basePath/.gsd         — fast path (common case)
   295	 *   2. git rev-parse root    — handles cwd-is-a-subdirectory
   296	 *   3. Walk up from basePath — handles moved .gsd in an ancestor (bounded by git root)
   297	 *   4. basePath/.gsd         — creation fallback (init scenario)
   298	 *
   299	 * Result is cached per basePath for the process lifetime.
   300	 */
   301	export function gsdRoot(basePath: string): string {
   302	  const cached = gsdRootCache.get(basePath);
   303	  if (cached) return cached;
   304	
   305	  const result = probeGsdRoot(basePath);
   306	  gsdRootCache.set(basePath, result);
   307	  return result;
   308	}
   309	
   310	function probeGsdRoot(rawBasePath: string): string {
   311	  // 1. Fast path — check the input path directly
   312	  const local = join(rawBasePath, ".gsd");
   313	  if (existsSync(local)) return local;
   314	
   315	  // Resolve symlinks so path comparisons work correctly across platforms
   316	  // (e.g. macOS /var → /private/var). Use rawBasePath as fallback if not resolvable.
   317	  let basePath: string;
   318	  try { basePath = realpathSync.native(rawBasePath); } catch { basePath = rawBasePath; }
   319	
   320	  // 2. Git root anchor — used as both probe target and walk-up boundary

     1	/**
     2	 * Remote Questions Config Helper
     3	 *
     4	 * Extracted from remote-questions extension so onboarding.ts can import
     5	 * it without crossing the compiled/uncompiled boundary. The extension
     6	 * files in src/resources/ are shipped as raw .ts and loaded via jiti,
     7	 * but onboarding.ts is compiled by tsc — dynamic imports from compiled
     8	 * JS to uncompiled .ts fail at runtime (#592).
     9	 */
    10	
    11	import { existsSync, readFileSync, writeFileSync, mkdirSync } from "node:fs";
    12	import { dirname, join } from "node:path";
    13	import { appRoot } from "./app-paths.js";
    14	
    15	// Inlined from preferences.ts to avoid crossing the compiled/uncompiled
    16	// boundary — this file is compiled by tsc, but preferences.ts is loaded
    17	// via jiti at runtime. Importing it as .js fails because no .js exists
    18	// in dist/. See #592, #1110.
    19	const GLOBAL_PREFERENCES_PATH = join(appRoot, "preferences.md");
    20	
    21	export function saveRemoteQuestionsConfig(channel: "slack" | "discord" | "telegram", channelId: string): void {
    22	  const prefsPath = GLOBAL_PREFERENCES_PATH;
    23	  const block = [
    24	    "remote_questions:",
    25	    `  channel: ${channel}`,
    26	    `  channel_id: "${channelId}"`,
    27	    "  timeout_minutes: 5",
    28	    "  poll_interval_seconds: 5",
    29	  ].join("\n");
    30	
    31	  const content = existsSync(prefsPath) ? readFileSync(prefsPath, "utf-8") : "";
    32	  const fmMatch = content.match(/^---\n([\s\S]*?)\n---/);
    33	  let next = content;
    34	
    35	  if (fmMatch) {
    36	    let frontmatter = fmMatch[1];
    37	    const regex = /remote_questions:[\s\S]*?(?=\n[a-zA-Z_]|\n---|$)/;
    38	    frontmatter = regex.test(frontmatter) ? frontmatter.replace(regex, block) : `${frontmatter.trimEnd()}\n${block}`;
    39	    next = `---\n${frontmatter}\n---${content.slice(fmMatch[0].length)}`;
    40	  } else {
    41	    next = `---\n${block}\n---\n\n${content}`;
    42	  }
    43	
    44	  mkdirSync(dirname(prefsPath), { recursive: true });
    45	  writeFileSync(prefsPath, next, "utf-8");
    46	}
    47

   768	export async function ensurePreferencesFile(
   769	  path: string,
   770	  ctx: ExtensionCommandContext,
   771	  scope: "global" | "project",
   772	): Promise<void> {
   773	  if (!existsSync(path)) {
   774	    const template = await loadFile(join(dirname(fileURLToPath(import.meta.url)), "templates", "preferences.md"));
   775	    if (!template) {
   776	      ctx.ui.notify("Could not load GSD preferences template.", "error");
   777	      return;
   778	    }
   779	    await saveFile(path, template);
   780	    ctx.ui.notify(`Created ${scope} GSD skill preferences at ${path}`, "info");
   781	  } else {
   782	    ctx.ui.notify(`Using existing ${scope} GSD skill preferences at ${path}`, "info");
   783	  }

    25	/** Extract body content after frontmatter closing delimiter, or null if none. */
    26	function extractBodyAfterFrontmatter(content: string): string | null {
    27	  const closingIdx = content.indexOf("\n---", content.indexOf("---"));
    28	  if (closingIdx === -1) return null;
    29	  const afterFrontmatter = content.slice(closingIdx + 4);
    30	  return afterFrontmatter.trim() ? afterFrontmatter : null;
    31	}

    36	function tryParseInteger(val: string): number | null {
    37	  return /^\d+$/.test(val) ? Number(val) : null;
    38	}

    40	/** Parse a string as a finite number, or return null on failure. */
    41	function tryParseNumber(val: string): number | null {
    42	  const n = Number(val);
    43	  return !isNaN(n) && isFinite(n) ? n : null;
    44	}
    45	
    46	/** Parse a string as a number in the 0–100 range, or return null on failure. */
    47	function tryParsePercentage(val: string): number | null {
    48	  const n = Number(val);
    49	  return !isNaN(n) && n >= 0 && n <= 100 ? n : null;
    50	}

   109	
   110	export async function handleImportClaude(ctx: ExtensionCommandContext, scope: "global" | "project"): Promise<void> {
   111	  const path = scope === "project" ? getProjectGSDPreferencesPath() : getGlobalGSDPreferencesPath();
   112	  if (!existsSync(path)) {
   113	    await ensurePreferencesFile(path, ctx, scope);
   114	  }
   115	
   116	  const readPrefs = (): Record<string, unknown> => {
   117	    if (!existsSync(path)) return { version: 1 };
   118	    const content = readFileSync(path, "utf-8");
   119	    const [frontmatterLines] = splitFrontmatter(content);
   120	    return frontmatterLines ? parseFrontmatterMap(frontmatterLines) : { version: 1 };
   121	  };
   122	
   123	  const writePrefs = async (prefs: Record<string, unknown>): Promise<void> => {
   124	    prefs.version = prefs.version || 1;
   125	    const frontmatter = serializePreferencesToFrontmatter(prefs);
   126	    let body = "\n# GSD Skill Preferences\n\nSee `~/.gsd/agent/extensions/gsd/docs/preferences-reference.md` for full field documentation and examples.\n";
   127	    if (existsSync(path)) {
   128	      const preserved = extractBodyAfterFrontmatter(readFileSync(path, "utf-8"));
   129	      if (preserved) body = preserved;
   130	    }
   131	    await saveFile(path, `---\n${frontmatter}---${body}`);
   132	  };
   133	
   134	  await runClaudeImportFlow(ctx, scope, readPrefs, writePrefs);
   135	}
   136	
   137	export async function handlePrefsMode(ctx: ExtensionCommandContext, scope: "global" | "project"): Promise<void> {
   138	  const path = scope === "project" ? getProjectGSDPreferencesPath() : getGlobalGSDPreferencesPath();
   139	  const existing = scope === "project" ? loadProjectGSDPreferences() : loadGlobalGSDPreferences();
   140	  const prefs: Record<string, unknown> = existing?.preferences ? { ...existing.preferences } : {};
   141	
   142	  await configureMode(ctx, prefs);
   143	
   144	  // Serialize and save
   145	  prefs.version = prefs.version || 1;
   146	  const frontmatter = serializePreferencesToFrontmatter(prefs);
   147	
   148	  let body = "\n# GSD Skill Preferences\n\nSee `~/.gsd/agent/extensions/gsd/docs/preferences-reference.md` for full field documentation and examples.\n";
   149	  if (existsSync(path)) {
   150	    const preserved = extractBodyAfterFrontmatter(readFileSync(path, "utf-8"));
   151	    if (preserved) body = preserved;
   152	  }
   153	
   154	  const content = `---\n${frontmatter}---${body}`;
   155	  await saveFile(path, content);
   156	  await ctx.waitForIdle();
   157	  await ctx.reload();
   158	  ctx.ui.notify(`Saved ${scope} preferences to ${path}`, "info");
   159	}

   606	async function configureAdvanced(ctx: ExtensionCommandContext, prefs: Record<string, unknown>): Promise<void> {
   607	  const currentUnique = prefs.unique_milestone_ids;
   608	  const uniqueChoice = await ctx.ui.select(
   609	    `Unique milestone IDs${currentUnique !== undefined ? ` (current: ${currentUnique})` : ""}:`,
   610	    ["true", "false", "(keep current)"],
   611	  );
   612	  if (uniqueChoice && uniqueChoice !== "(keep current)") {
   613	    prefs.unique_milestone_ids = uniqueChoice === "true";
   614	  }
   615	}

   617	// ─── Main wizard with category menu ─────────────────────────────────────────
   618	
   619	export async function handlePrefsWizard(
   620	  ctx: ExtensionCommandContext,
   621	  scope: "global" | "project",
   622	): Promise<void> {
   623	  const path = scope === "project" ? getProjectGSDPreferencesPath() : getGlobalGSDPreferencesPath();
   624	  const existing = scope === "project" ? loadProjectGSDPreferences() : loadGlobalGSDPreferences();
   625	  const prefs: Record<string, unknown> = existing?.preferences ? { ...existing.preferences } : {};
   626	
   627	  ctx.ui.notify(`GSD preferences (${scope}) — pick a category to configure.`, "info");
   628	
   629	  while (true) {
   630	    const summaries = buildCategorySummaries(prefs);
   631	    const options = [
   632	      `Workflow Mode   ${summaries.mode}`,
   633	      `Models          ${summaries.models}`,
   634	      `Timeouts        ${summaries.timeouts}`,
   635	      `Git             ${summaries.git}`,
   636	      `Skills          ${summaries.skills}`,
   637	      `Budget          ${summaries.budget}`,
   638	      `Notifications   ${summaries.notifications}`,
   639	      `Advanced        ${summaries.advanced}`,
   640	      `── Save & Exit ──`,
   641	    ];
   642	
   643	    const raw = await ctx.ui.select("GSD Preferences", options);
   644	    const choice = typeof raw === "string" ? raw : "";
   645	    if (!choice || choice.includes("Save & Exit")) break;
   646	
   647	    if (choice.startsWith("Workflow Mode"))      await configureMode(ctx, prefs);
   648	    else if (choice.startsWith("Models"))        await configureModels(ctx, prefs);
   649	    else if (choice.startsWith("Timeouts"))      await configureTimeouts(ctx, prefs);
   650	    else if (choice.startsWith("Git"))           await configureGit(ctx, prefs);
   651	    else if (choice.startsWith("Skills"))        await configureSkills(ctx, prefs);
   652	    else if (choice.startsWith("Budget"))        await configureBudget(ctx, prefs);
   653	    else if (choice.startsWith("Notifications")) await configureNotifications(ctx, prefs);
   654	    else if (choice.startsWith("Advanced"))      await configureAdvanced(ctx, prefs);
   655	  }
   656	
   657	  // ─── Serialize to frontmatter ───────────────────────────────────────────
   658	  prefs.version = prefs.version || 1;
   659	  const frontmatter = serializePreferencesToFrontmatter(prefs);
   660	
   661	  // Preserve existing body content (everything after closing ---)
   662	  let body = "\n# GSD Skill Preferences\n\nSee `~/.gsd/agent/extensions/gsd/docs/preferences-reference.md` for full field documentation and examples.\n";
   663	  if (existsSync(path)) {
   664	    const preserved = extractBodyAfterFrontmatter(readFileSync(path, "utf-8"));
   665	    if (preserved) body = preserved;
   666	  }
   667	
   668	  const content = `---\n${frontmatter}---${body}`;
   669	
   670	  await saveFile(path, content);
   671	  await ctx.waitForIdle();
   672	  await ctx.reload();
   673	  ctx.ui.notify(`Saved ${scope} preferences to ${path}`, "info");
   674	}
   675	
   676	/** Wrap a YAML value in double quotes if it contains special characters. */
   677	export function yamlSafeString(val: unknown): string {
   678	  if (typeof val !== "string") return String(val);
   679	  if (/[:#{\[\]'"`,|>&*!?@%]/.test(val) || val.trim() !== val || val === "") {
   680	    return `"${val.replace(/\\/g, "\\\\").replace(/"/g, '\\"')}"`;
   681	  }
   682	  return val;
   683	}

   722	/**
   723	 * Check if this is the very first time GSD has been used on this machine.
   724	 * Returns true if ~/.gsd/ doesn't exist or has no preferences or auth.
   725	 */
   726	export function isFirstEverLaunch(): boolean {
   727	  if (!existsSync(gsdHome)) return true;
   728	
   729	  // If we have preferences, not first launch
   730	  if (
   731	    existsSync(join(gsdHome, "preferences.md")) ||
   732	    existsSync(join(gsdHome, "PREFERENCES.md"))
   733	  ) {
   734	    return false;
   735	  }
   736	
   737	  // If we have auth.json, not first launch (onboarding.ts already ran)
   738	  if (existsSync(join(gsdHome, "agent", "auth.json"))) return false;
   739	
   740	  // Check legacy path too
   741	  const legacyPath = join(homedir(), ".pi", "agent", "gsd-preferences.md");
   742	  if (existsSync(legacyPath)) return false;
   743	
   744	  return true;
   745	}

import { mkdtempSync, mkdirSync, writeFileSync, rmSync, statSync } from 'node:fs';
import { tmpdir } from 'node:os';
import { join } from 'node:path';

const tmp = mkdtempSync(join(tmpdir(), 'gsd-pref-case-'));
process.env.GSD_HOME = join(tmp, 'home');
mkdirSync(process.env.GSD_HOME, { recursive: true });
writeFileSync(join(process.env.GSD_HOME, 'preferences.md'), '---\nmode: solo\n---\n');
writeFileSync(join(process.env.GSD_HOME, 'PREFERENCES.md'), '---\nmode: team\n---\n');

const project = join(tmp, 'project');
mkdirSync(join(project, '.gsd'), { recursive: true });
writeFileSync(join(project, '.gsd', 'preferences.md'), '---\nmode: solo\n---\n');
writeFileSync(join(project, '.gsd', 'PREFERENCES.md'), '---\nmode: team\n---\n');
process.chdir(project);

const prefs = await import('/testbed/src/resources/extensions/gsd/preferences.ts');
const gitignore = await import('/testbed/src/resources/extensions/gsd/gitignore.ts');

const failures = [];
const global = prefs.loadGlobalGSDPreferences();
const projectPrefs = prefs.loadProjectGSDPreferences();
if (!prefs.getGlobalGSDPreferencesPath().endsWith('PREFERENCES.md')) failures.push(`global getter not canonical uppercase: ${prefs.getGlobalGSDPreferencesPath()}`);
if (!prefs.getProjectGSDPreferencesPath().endsWith('PREFERENCES.md')) failures.push(`project getter not canonical uppercase: ${prefs.getProjectGSDPreferencesPath()}`);
if (!global?.path.endsWith('PREFERENCES.md') || global.preferences.mode !== 'team') failures.push(`global load did not prefer uppercase: ${global?.path} ${global?.preferences.mode}`);
if (!projectPrefs?.path.endsWith('PREFERENCES.md') || projectPrefs.preferences.mode !== 'team') failures.push(`project load did not prefer uppercase: ${projectPrefs?.path} ${projectPrefs?.preferences.mode}`);

const fresh = join(tmp, 'fresh');
mkdirSync(fresh, { recursive: true });
gitignore.ensurePreferences(fresh);
const created = join(fresh, '.gsd', 'PREFERENCES.md');
try { statSync(created); } catch { failures.push(`ensurePreferences did not create ${created}`); }

rmSync(tmp, { recursive: true, force: true });
if (failures.length) {
  console.error(failures.join('\n'));
  process.exit(1);
}
console.log('ok');

   200	export function ensurePreferences(basePath) {
   201	    const preferencesPath = join(gsdRoot(basePath), "preferences.md");
   202	    const legacyPath = join(gsdRoot(basePath), "PREFERENCES.md");
   203	    if (existsSync(preferencesPath) || existsSync(legacyPath)) {

   218	# GSD Skill Preferences
   219	
   220	Project-specific guidance for skill selection and execution preferences.
   221	
   222	See \`~/.gsd/agent/extensions/gsd/docs/preferences-reference.md\` for full field documentation and examples.
   223	
   224	## Fields
   225	
   226	- \`always_use_skills\`: Skills that must be available during all GSD operations
   227	- \`prefer_skills\`: Skills to prioritize when multiple options exist
   228	- \`avoid_skills\`: Skills to minimize or avoid (with lower priority than prefer)
   229	- \`skill_rules\`: Context-specific rules (e.g., "use tool X for Y type of work")
   230	- \`custom_instructions\`: Append-only project guidance (do not override system rules)
   231	- \`models\`: Model preferences for specific task types
   232	- \`skill_discovery\`: Automatic skill detection preferences
   233	- \`auto_supervisor\`: Supervision and gating rules for autonomous modes

     9	import { join, dirname } from "node:path";
    10	import { fileURLToPath } from "node:url";
    11	import { getGlobalGSDPreferencesPath, getLegacyGlobalGSDPreferencesPath, getProjectGSDPreferencesPath, loadGlobalGSDPreferences, loadProjectGSDPreferences, loadEffectiveGSDPreferences, resolveAllSkillReferences, } from "./preferences.js";
    12	import { loadFile, saveFile, splitFrontmatter, parseFrontmatterMap } from "./files.js";
    13	import { runClaudeImportFlow } from "./claude-import.js";
    14	/** Extract body content after frontmatter closing delimiter, or null if none. */
    15	function extractBodyAfterFrontmatter(content) {
    16	    const closingIdx = content.indexOf("\n---", content.indexOf("---"));
    17	    if (closingIdx === -1)
    18	        return null;
    19	    const afterFrontmatter = content.slice(closingIdx + 4);
    20	    return afterFrontmatter.trim() ? afterFrontmatter : null;
    21	}
    22	// ─── Numeric validation helpers ──────────────────────────────────────────────
    23	/** Parse a string as a non-negative integer, or return null on failure. */
    24	function tryParseInteger(val) {
    25	    return /^\d+$/.test(val) ? Number(val) : null;
    26	}
    27	/** Parse a string as a finite number, or return null on failure. */
    28	function tryParseNumber(val) {
    29	    const n = Number(val);
    30	    return !isNaN(n) && isFinite(n) ? n : null;
    31	}
    32	/** Parse a string as a number in the 0–100 range, or return null on failure. */
    33	function tryParsePercentage(val) {
    34	    const n = Number(val);
    35	    return !isNaN(n) && n >= 0 && n <= 100 ? n : null;
    36	}
    37	export async function handlePrefs(args, ctx) {
    38	    const trimmed = args.trim();
    39	    if (trimmed === "" || trimmed === "global" || trimmed === "wizard" || trimmed === "setup"
    40	        || trimmed === "wizard global" || trimmed === "setup global") {
    41	        await ensurePreferencesFile(getGlobalGSDPreferencesPath(), ctx, "global");
    42	        await handlePrefsWizard(ctx, "global");
    43	        return;
    44	    }
    45	    if (trimmed === "project" || trimmed === "wizard project" || trimmed === "setup project") {
    46	        await ensurePreferencesFile(getProjectGSDPreferencesPath(), ctx, "project");
    47	        await handlePrefsWizard(ctx, "project");
    48	        return;
    49	    }
    50	    if (trimmed === "import-claude" || trimmed === "import-claude global") {
    51	        await handleImportClaude(ctx, "global");
    52	        return;
    53	    }
    54	    if (trimmed === "import-claude project") {
    55	        await handleImportClaude(ctx, "project");
    56	        return;
    57	    }
    58	    if (trimmed === "status") {
    59	        const globalPrefs = loadGlobalGSDPreferences();
    60	        const projectPrefs = loadProjectGSDPreferences();
    61	        const canonicalGlobal = getGlobalGSDPreferencesPath();
    62	        const legacyGlobal = getLegacyGlobalGSDPreferencesPath();
    63	        const globalStatus = globalPrefs
    64	            ? `present: ${globalPrefs.path}${globalPrefs.path === legacyGlobal ? " (legacy fallback)" : ""}`
    65	            : `missing: ${canonicalGlobal}`;
    66	        const projectStatus = projectPrefs ? `present: ${projectPrefs.path}` : `missing: ${getProjectGSDPreferencesPath()}`;
    67	        const lines = [`GSD skill prefs — global ${globalStatus}; project ${projectStatus}`];
    68	        const effective = loadEffectiveGSDPreferences();
    69	        let hasUnresolved = false;
    70	        if (effective) {
    71	            const report = resolveAllSkillReferences(effective.preferences, process.cwd());
    72	            const resolved = [...report.resolutions.values()].filter(r => r.method !== "unresolved");
    73	            hasUnresolved = report.warnings.length > 0;
    74	            if (resolved.length > 0 || hasUnresolved) {
    75	                lines.push(`Skills: ${resolved.length} resolved, ${report.warnings.length} unresolved`);
    76	            }
    77	            if (hasUnresolved) {
    78	                lines.push(`Unresolved: ${report.warnings.join(", ")}`);
    79	            }
    80	        }
    81	        ctx.ui.notify(lines.join("\n"), hasUnresolved ? "warning" : "info");
    82	        return;
    83	    }
    84	    ctx.ui.notify("Usage: /gsd prefs [global|project|status|wizard|setup|import-claude [global|project]]", "info");
    85	}
    86	export async function handleImportClaude(ctx, scope) {
    87	    const path = scope === "project" ? getProjectGSDPreferencesPath() : getGlobalGSDPreferencesPath();
    88	    if (!existsSync(path)) {
    89	        await ensurePreferencesFile(path, ctx, scope);
    90	    }
    91	    const readPrefs = () => {
    92	        if (!existsSync(path))
    93	            return { version: 1 };
    94	        const content = readFileSync(path, "utf-8");
    95	        const [frontmatterLines] = splitFrontmatter(content);
    96	        return frontmatterLines ? parseFrontmatterMap(frontmatterLines) : { version: 1 };
    97	    };
    98	    const writePrefs = async (prefs) => {
    99	        prefs.version = prefs.version || 1;
   100	        const frontmatter = serializePreferencesToFrontmatter(prefs);
   101	        let body = "\n# GSD Skill Preferences\n\nSee `~/.gsd/agent/extensions/gsd/docs/preferences-reference.md` for full field documentation and examples.\n";
   102	        if (existsSync(path)) {
   103	            const preserved = extractBodyAfterFrontmatter(readFileSync(path, "utf-8"));
   104	            if (preserved)
   105	                body = preserved;
   106	        }
   107	        await saveFile(path, `---\n${frontmatter}---${body}`);
   108	    };
   109	    await runClaudeImportFlow(ctx, scope, readPrefs, writePrefs);
   110	}
   111	export async function handlePrefsMode(ctx, scope) {
   112	    const path = scope === "project" ? getProjectGSDPreferencesPath() : getGlobalGSDPreferencesPath();
   113	    const existing = scope === "project" ? loadProjectGSDPreferences() : loadGlobalGSDPreferences();
   114	    const prefs = existing?.preferences ? { ...existing.preferences } : {};
   115	    await configureMode(ctx, prefs);
   116	    // Serialize and save
   117	    prefs.version = prefs.version || 1;
   118	    const frontmatter = serializePreferencesToFrontmatter(prefs);
   119	    let body = "\n# GSD Skill Preferences\n\nSee `~/.gsd/agent/extensions/gsd/docs/preferences-reference.md` for full field documentation and examples.\n";
   120	    if (existsSync(path)) {
   121	        const preserved = extractBodyAfterFrontmatter(readFileSync(path, "utf-8"));
   122	        if (preserved)
   123	            body = preserved;
   124	    }
   125	    const content = `---\n${frontmatter}---${body}`;
   126	    await saveFile(path, content);
   127	    await ctx.waitForIdle();
   128	    await ctx.reload();
   129	    ctx.ui.notify(`Saved ${scope} preferences to ${path}`, "info");
   130	}

    12	import { appRoot } from "./app-paths.js";

    16	// in dist/. See #592, #1110.

    19	    const prefsPath = GLOBAL_PREFERENCES_PATH;
    20	    const block = [

    22	        `  channel: ${channel}`,
    23	        `  channel_id: "${channelId}"`,
    24	        "  timeout_minutes: 5",
    25	        "  poll_interval_seconds: 5",
    26	    ].join("\n");

+function getLoadedPreferencesPath(scope: "global" | "project"): string | null {

+function getLoadedPreferencesPath(scope: "global" | "project"): string | null {
